Before he finished speaking, a dispirited young farmer said, "He bathes naked by the well and runs into the courtyard naked, scaring the women from coming out." Another farmer said, "He bullies us terribly. He is probably an official. He is the one standing with his thighs exposed in the front. Sir, you saw him, didn't you? The one who came before was Takahashi. After Takahashi left, he came. He is extremely fierce." I asked what his name was, but no one knew. I told our group that we had come from Nanjing specifically to investigate this matter. A farmer's face seemed to show a hint of comfort. At that moment, a light rain suddenly started. We bid farewell and had lunch at the Xing residence in the front village. I asked Section staff member Guo, and then I learned that the terrifying figure in the farmers' mouths was Kato, the assistant police inspector (equivalent to our country's patrol officer) who had guided us and was naked.

(V) Mr. Xing's Remarks

While waiting for lunch at the Xing residence, I asked the host, Mr. Xing, about the cause of the incident. Mr. Xing was in his thirties, with a square face and narrowed eyes. He wore a blue jacket and trousers and was barefoot in his shoes. He was talkative and relatively open-minded. He said, "In the second lunar month of this year, many Koreans suddenly came and kowtowed to the river, claiming to be worshiping the river and breaking ground. We then learned that Hao Yongde was leading Koreans to plant rice in the Jiangjia Wobao area (twenty li away from here) and was digging trenches. But at that time, they only broke ground and did not dig trenches. Until March, they actually started digging. They dug from Jiangjia Wobao to the west and from the riverbank to the east.

Page 11

Continued Special

The residents of our second district gathered to resist and complained to the county government and the municipal office. On the sixteenth day of the fourth lunar month, Police Chief Lu came with soldiers. The Koreans agreed not to dig. The next day, they went back on their word. Lu detained ten Koreans. On the eighteenth, Lu came again, and Captain Tang also came. The Japanese police then joined the Koreans on that day. Lu left without result. At the end of the fourth lunar month, Chinese and Japanese officials came to investigate. The Japanese police withdrew and then came again. On the seventeenth day of the fifth lunar month (that is, July 1st of the Gregorian calendar), our side gathered more than four hundred people and started leveling the trench at noon on that day. Because of the interference of the Japanese police, a dispute arose. In the evening, Japanese police officer Takahashi said to our representatives, "The more of you come tomorrow, the better. Bring more guns, or prepare more coffins. Tomorrow, two thousand Japanese soldiers will come with machine guns and cannons, waiting for you." The next day, our side gathered more than one hundred people, mostly carrying guns for self-defense. Some could even shoot down solitary birds. More than twenty Japanese soldiers came. Our side started leveling the trench in the morning. The Japanese police pulled our farmers, but they were snatched back by our side. On that day, Police Sub-Inspector Nakagawa, wearing white clothes and a black beard, fired the first shot. Our side also retaliated. The Japanese fired east along the river, and our side shot from the west of the bridge. Then, I entered the He residence and used the artillery platform for cover. The shooting started at 8:00 AM and lasted until 10:00 AM, about two hours. Both sides fired blanks, so there were no casualties. After that, our government stopped leveling the trench, and the number of Japanese soldiers increased to more than forty. Although the number of Japanese soldiers has decreased recently, they still fired guns yesterday to show their power." I asked, "Has anyone talked about paying rent for the land that has been dug up?" Xing replied, "Although there is such talk, it has not been realized." "Who fired the first shot?" "It was definitely Nakagawa from the Japanese side." ( ) "Are there still any Koreans here?" "Only the four who cook for the Japanese. The rest are all in the Jiangjia Wobao area." "Have the Japanese police ever been stationed in this village?" "Not yet." "Has the Yitong River ever flooded before?" "It floods often. Sir, haven't you seen the water bubble in front of the door? The land along the river is low-lying, so there are floods every two or three years." "How much land does the trench occupy?" "About forty mu. The land of the Mu and Sun families has been dug up." At this point, lunch was served. The vegetables and rice were delicious.

(VI) Some Trivial News

Hardship is High. I heard that the rice planted by the Koreans is less than an inch tall and mostly dried up. Those living near Wanbaoshan have difficulty finding food and steal bean leaves at night to fill their stomachs. Their situation is extremely difficult.

Pregnant Woman. A Yu surname woman living in Shaokou, 25 years old, was about to give birth when two Japanese soldiers suddenly entered the courtyard, making a lot of noise. The woman was frightened, and the baby could not be delivered and died two days later. She is a victim of the Wanbaoshan incident, but no one outside knows about it.

Impersonating a Reporter. A Chinese police officer named Tian, brought by the Japanese side, often goes to the countryside posing as a Dongbao newspaper reporter from this port to gather information. The farmers believe him to be true and often tell him the real situation, hoping that he will speak out for them. Who would have thought that he is Chinese in appearance but Japanese at heart? During the shooting, a bullet passed over his scalp, and he has not come back since. The farmers all say that this is a warning from heaven.

(VII) Returning in the Rain

At 3:30 PM that afternoon, we left the Xing residence and returned to the city. When we reached Shuiquan, a heavy rain suddenly came, pouring down. Except for me, who was holding an umbrella, everyone was soaked in the rain. Professor Zhang Qiyun took off his clothes in a civilian's house, wearing only a woolen blanket. I sat in the back of the cart, holding an umbrella to cover him. We couldn't help but laugh at each other. We arrived in the city after 7:00 PM. I and a Zhongda student met with Chief Zhou of the Municipal Office to express our gratitude. Zhou asked about the local situation in detail and gave us a map recently made by the office (as shown in Figure 3). By following the map, everything was clear at a glance. It is attached in reduced size for the readers' reference.

(VIII) Conclusion

During my one-day visit to Majia Shaokou, I investigated the situation of the Japanese soldiers' intrusion into the interior. What I saw was shocking and filled me with emotion. Summarizing what I saw and heard, there are several things that the readers should pay attention to: (1) The eighteen Chinese li waterway from Majia Shaokou to Kuanghuangtun is leased for five hundred qing, with a lease term of ten years (according to the contract). Such a long waterway, such a wide paddy field, and such a long period of time are truly a major economic endeavor, different from the rice planting of ordinary Koreans in various places. (2) The land on both sides of the eighteen-li-long waterway is all good farmland. I investigated the soil quality, which is loose and easily cracked. When the Yitong River rises, not only will the land along the river be damaged, but also the fields along the trenches will be in danger of collapsing. Because the trenches have no trees and the soil is loose, the banks will inevitably collapse, making it difficult to maintain the current straight length. (3) The July 2nd incident was provoked by Takahashi and guided by Nakagawa. If there had been no threats from Takahashi (according to Xing's remarks), the farmers would not have brought guns. If there had been no shooting by Nakagawa, the farmers would not have retaliated. The responsibility in this is clear, and I ask the people of the country to pay attention. (4) The Japanese soldiers occupy Majia Shaokou as if it were a forbidden area, intruding into civilian houses and acting like occupiers. Their activities have gone beyond the treaty. Therefore, the Wanbaoshan incident has expanded from the economic relationship between Chinese and Korean farmers to the treaty relationship between China and Japan. (5) In recent days, newspapers in various places have reported the removal of Japanese police. This visit proves that as of August 1st, the fact and preparation for the Japanese police to withdraw had not taken place. The Japanese police have been stationed at Majia Shaokou since the eighteenth day of the fourth lunar month (according to Mr. Xing), and as of August 1st of the Gregorian calendar, they have occupied it for more than two months.

I am a teacher of twelve years, and I am ashamed to have made little contribution to the country and society. The Wanbaoshan incident has caused me great concern. Taking advantage of my free time during the summer vacation, I made this trip and recorded what I saw and heard, publishing it to the public. It is nothing more than fulfilling my duty to society as a citizen, without any mission or expectation. This should be stated. (Published on August 4th at Changchun School)

Figure 3

Legend: Railway Station, Paddy Field, Field, Village, Town, Road, Canal, Mountain, Water Bubble, Bridge, Dam, District, Lingkou, Local Land, Railway Bridge.

Description:

1. The trench dug from Majia Shaokou to the Jiangjia Wobao farming office is about twenty li long.

2. The trench dug at Majia Shaokou is about three zhang wide and one zhang deep. The earth piled on both sides is about five zhang wide, occupying the people's land about eight zhang wide. The depth, shallowness, width, and narrowness of the trenches are unequal. The occupied people's land, excluding the weeds and old ditches, occupies about forty mu of good farmland.

3. The dam is about four zhang wide and one zhang five cun high, all made of willow branches. The dam is piled up with soil, leaving a place for the water to flow. If the place for the water to flow is filled with soil bags, the river will be cut off, and the water will flow directly into the ditch.

4. The ferry has been stopped, and river transportation is not possible. It is quite difficult to pass through on both sides.

Important News

The 154th Regular Meeting of the Central Committee

Revised Article 6 of the Election Law for the Fourth National Congress

The Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang held its 154th regular meeting in the first conference hall of the Central Party Headquarters at 8:00 AM today (the 13th). Those present were Zhu Peide, Yu Youren, Ye Chucang, and Ding Weifen. Those attending as observers were Wang Boqun, Chen Bulei, Wang Zhengting, Ke Xing'e, Miao Peicheng, Yu Jingtang, Fang Juehui, Zeng Yangfu, and Jiao Yitang. Chairman Zhu Peide resolved the following cases. (1) Revised Article 6, Item A of the Election Law for Representatives of the Fourth National Congress, as "The Central Committee shall propose a number of candidates for representatives from each province or special municipality. The primary election representatives shall elect half or more than half of the number of representatives from each province or special municipality from this group of candidates. The remaining representatives shall be freely elected by the primary election representatives." (2) Approved Qin Yiwen, Li Hanming, Deng Jiyu, Liu Youting, and Zhang Zichu as executive members of the Qingdao Special City Party Department, and Qiu Zhiqing, Fan Chunyang, and Wang Puquan as alternate executive members. (3) Approved the resignation of Zhang Jinjian, a preparatory member of the Wu Chang Zhu Ping Railway Special Party Department, and appointed Shu Songsheng to replace him. (4) Zhang Zhenhan and Ding Zhipan, preparatory members of the Special Party Department of the 48th Division of the Army, were transferred, and Miao Songpei and Yang Shaodong were appointed to replace them. (5) Revised the Regulations on the Examination of Popular Speakers and passed the Organizational Regulations of the Examination Committee for Popular Speakers. (6) The Central Supervisory Committee sent a case to punish a party member. Zhang Rusong of Jiande, Zhejiang, was expelled from the party for one year. The resolution was approved. (7) Still recommended Committee Member Chen Lifu to attend the Central Memorial Week report next Monday.

Wanbaoshan

The Japanese Police Have Officially Withdrawn

The Koreans also have the intention of leaving

According to news from the Changchun Municipal Office, the Japanese police who shielded the Korean farmers and forcibly dug the dam have been protested by the Municipal Preparatory Office many times and have all been withdrawn. The Japanese Consul Tashi Shigetoku has not followed suit. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs officially sent a note to the Japanese Ambassador to China on July 22, ordering the Japanese police to withdraw and the Korean farmers to leave. On the 23rd, Special Commissioner Zhong and Japanese Consul-General to Jilin Ishii Jutaro discussed the withdrawal of the Japanese police and further negotiated the case. Ishii telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for instructions, which have been approved and forwarded to the Changchun Japanese Consul Tashi for compliance. On August 2, Special Commissioner Zhong returned to Jilin from Liaoning. On the same day, Tashi went to Jilin to discuss with Ishii the postponement of the withdrawal. The next day, he returned to Changchun but did not comply. With the urging of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Chinese Embassy in Japan, and Special Commissioner Zhong in Jilin, Tashi finally sent Kuraoto Hideaki, the head of the consulate, to officially declare to the Changchun Municipal Preparatory Office on August 6 that the police would be withdrawn on the 8th. He also said that he would go there the next day to supervise the complete withdrawal. On the 7th, the Jilin Provincial Government sent Zhang Qingyun to investigate the actual situation, and the Municipal Preparatory Office sent Zhou Wuxiang, He Rongchang, and Wei Ronghou to accompany him to inspect everything. On the 8th, at Chenshi (7-9 AM), they left Changchun. At 6:00 PM, the Municipal Preparatory Office received a telephone call from the office, reporting that a total of 26 Japanese police officers, carrying 26 large guns and one machine gun, lived in He's house at Majia Shaokou and in the military tents along the river. They took eight large carts and were led by Kuraoto Hideaki to withdraw into the city at 1:00 PM. Twelve Koreans followed behind. The remaining twenty or so households, about sixty men, women, and children, in Jiangjia Wobao and Zhang Hongbin's courtyard. Before leaving, Kuraoto told Cao Longbiao, the director of the Third Branch Bureau of Changchun County, that if these Koreans wanted to go elsewhere, they should be allowed to do so. The food in that area was all transported from the city, and the farmers would not sell it to them. The Japanese Consulate in Jilin has repeatedly received letters from anti-Japanese Koreans, ordering the Koreans in Wanbaoshan to quickly withdraw, otherwise there will be a final disposition. The Koreans there had indicated one or two months ago that they would leave immediately after the Japanese police withdrew. It is expected that the Koreans there will all leave soon. The withdrawal of the Japanese police has been telegraphed by the Municipal Office to the Jilin Provincial Government, and Special Commissioner Zhong has telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Negotiations on this case are now underway. (August 8)

Shi Bu's Cavalry Continues to Arrive in Dezhou

The Deputy Department will be responsible for tens of thousands of dollars in accommodation fees.

The defeated soldiers will be reorganized into a division after being accommodated.

Jinan Correspondence: Shi Bu's defeated soldiers continue to retreat to northern Shandong in succession. According to reports from Dezhou, those who have arrived in the past two days are all in small, scattered groups, 30 people, 20 people, or 40 to 50 people. Their uniforms and weapons are incomplete. Yesterday (the 9th), a unit of cavalry also arrived. They are all accommodated by the reception center as soon as they arrive, and then immediately sent to Linyi. At 7:00 PM tonight (the 10th), the reporter visited Fan Pujiang, the representative of Deputy Zhang, and asked about Yan Xishan's arrival in Shanxi and the accommodation of Shi Bu's soldiers. According to him, Yan's return to Shanxi is a confirmed fact. Because Yan's father was ill, he had long planned to return home to visit him. The incident of Shi Yousan's mutiny happened to occur, and he was afraid of misunderstandings, so he did not immediately carry it out. Now that Shi's matter has been resolved, he has returned to Heshui Village to observe the situation. It seems that he has no role to play now, but it is impossible to predict what his future actions will be. Shi Yousan's defeated soldiers continue to arrive in Dezhou in small numbers in recent days. They must wait until they have all arrived before Chairman Han can submit a request to the Central Committee to stipulate the organization. The reception center established in Dezhou accommodates 100 when 100 arrive, and 80 when 80 arrive. It is expected that it will not exceed 10,000 people at most. The accommodation expenses, in addition to the 100,000 yuan undertaken by the Central Government, the Northeast can also undertake tens of thousands of yuan. The Northeast Army has stopped pursuing Shi Bu and will soon issue an order to return to their defense posts. As for Shi Bu, who has been accommodated in the Northeast, in addition to Shen Kequan's division, there are other small parts, the numbers of which are unknown. He will return to Ping tomorrow (the 12th), etc. According to Jiang Bocheng, the chief adviser of the Xingying General Headquarters, about 10,000 of Shi Bu's defeated soldiers have arrived in Shandong, and those who continue to come are only small scattered groups. They can be roughly organized into a division. Chairman Han has followed the orders of the Central Committee and sent Cheng Xixian and Tang Bangzhi to meet with General Commander Cao (Fulin) and Brigade Commander Li (Hanzhang) to be responsible for the compilation.

The Yellow River is Rising, the Situation is Serious

Both upstream and downstream telegraphed the province for help

And asked the River Affairs Bureau to allocate materials for emergency rescue

Jinan Correspondence: Continuous torrential rains have caused the Yellow River's water level to continue to rise. Both upstream Li Gong and downstream Tangjia have sent urgent alerts. The River Affairs Bureau has received telegrams from both upstream and downstream, and has reported to the Provincial Government. The telegrams are as follows:

Upstream Telegram: To Director Zhang of the Jinan River Affairs Bureau, yesterday (9th) afternoon, there was a torrential rain. The main current of Li Gong directly hit the dams such as 4, 9, and 10. The upper opening collapsed into the water. The protective embankment was completely submerged, only a foot above the water. I have ordered the guards to continue to build it up. The two defenses of the dam, which were previously built and reinforced as needed, are now submerged to the water level again and are still being built up with bricks. The lower corners of the ten dams and four embankments are submerged to the water level. The fifth embankment has been reinforced, and the two unreinforced embankments are again submerged to the water level. The sixth embankment is being reinforced, and the subsidence continues. The eighth embankment shows slight signs of subsidence. The new auxiliary dam base of the dam is submerged to the level of the embankment. The small embankments below the tenth dam have collapsed due to wind and waves and are uneven. I have ordered the nearby villages to send laborers to repair and defend them. In addition to urging the guards to do their best to reinforce the collapsed embankments, I am reporting this by telegram. Furthermore, the materials for Li Gong are now only twenty left. The current of Zhukou has not changed. Zhao Rongfu, Zhang Lufu, and Wang Huaiyi respectfully inform you.

Downstream Telegram: To Director Zhang of the Jinan River Affairs Bureau, the river water has increased by more than five chi. In many sections of this section, the embankments are level with the water, and some are submerged. The highest is less than one or two chi above the water. I have ordered all the guards and local short-term laborers in the whole section to quickly select and reinforce the stored materials such as straw and stones. I have also mobilized more than 200 farmers from nearby along the river to cut willows, transport stones, transport materials, and press down the soil to cooperate in the work to ensure safety. Recently, the materials have been exhausted, and the lower empty defense of the Tangjia East Dam is eight zhang long. The backflow is scouring it, and there is no embankment to protect it, so the bank collapsed three chi wide and eight zhang long, which is extremely dangerous. I have ordered Gao Fenfang, the defense commander, to supervise the farmers to use willow buildings to resist it. However, the engineering is dangerous everywhere. The autumn flood is in full swing, and there are no materials left in the entire section, which is very worrying. I beg you to add more materials such as straw and stones, and actively reinforce them, so as not to be negligent. Zhang Wenqing respectfully informs you.

Telegram to the Provincial Government: (1) To Chairman Han Jun of the Shandong Provincial Government, according to the telegrams from Zhang Lufu, Zhao Rongfu, and Wang Huaiyi of the first section in the south upstream, the continuous rainfall has caused the river water to rise sharply. The main current of the whole river is directly hitting the Li Gong Stone Dam. The lower corners of the fifth embankment of the dam, the upper corners of the seventh embankment, and the others have been submerged to the water level. The sixth and eighth embankments have subsided by one chi. The two defenses of the dam are still subsiding. We are now throwing soil and bricks, pressing down the engineering, and reinforcing them. We are actively protecting them and so on. In addition to telegraphed that the person to order and other supervised officer to take action force and protect, ensure safety, the actual for public convenience, Acting Shandong River Affairs Bureau Director Zhang Lianjia respectfully informs you. (Seal) (2) To Chairman Han Jun of the Shandong Provincial Government, I just received a telegram from Liang Jinming of the North Five section, the north five of the Zhang Wenqing- the civil officer on duty and the north five of the river branch office report officer Li FuChang- the two telegrams have been sent from Jinan, claiming that due to continuous rainy weather, the river water in the section continues to rise. The Tangjia East Section's the third 1, 2 embankments- the fast high waters are now running straight at the area so much of the 3 embankments is underwater. The Wangzaojia's 1st embankment or high up- the fast running waters and level on some embankments will be underwater etc. - other dams had the current moving against them and were always under the high waters as little as a foot or inches. now it appears the high waters are now rushing to get higher. We used the willow wood to support the the high banks as quick is needed. South four section of Yang ChengLin, Fengjia's second 23rd embankments through 33 embankments etc are only out of water by 8 or 9 inches Wang WangZhuang and other sections etc. some embankments the water is just to the level of the embankments. with the various dangers. Thus, and in another telegram the urgent reports from the officials have been telegraphed and please let us provide relief. acting director Zhang Lian Jia's stamp. (10th Day)

Post-Flood Relief in Xu-bu

Road and Telegraph Communications Fully Restored

Seven Refugee Shelters Established

Four Districts Delineated to Defend Against Yellow River Breaches

Quick dispatch from Xuzhou: The situation in Xu-bu on the 7th, with violent storms and rain and the potential for the old Yellow River course to flood the city, was detailed in a previous letter. The weather in this city cleared on the 9th, and the water in the old Yellow River course began to recede. However, along the riverbanks and in flooded areas within the city, many disaster victims were exposed to the elements, a truly pitiful sight. The Flood Relief Association is devising relief measures, which are detailed below. The flood within the city was primarily caused by the heavy rain. By the 9th, with the weather clearing, the water had begun to recede, but the ditches and drains were full, preventing drainage. To this day, some low-lying residences still have one or two feet of standing water, and clearing the ditches has not helped. Many people whose thatched houses collapsed still have no place to go. The water from the old Yellow River course, having breached bridges and roads, was not flowing smoothly downstream. Chen Xueshun, chief of the military and police supervision office, supervised the Seventh Division's engineers stationed in Xuzhou to excavate and facilitate the flow of water. The upstream water volume also decreased. Consequently, on the 9th and 10th, the water level receded by about one foot each day. The city of Xuzhou is now safe. Riverside residents sleeping on the roadsides are a common sight. After its establishment on the 8th, the Flood Relief Committee divided into departments. The county government is responsible for general affairs, the county party branch for relief work, and the office is located at the Property Management Office. As that office is still flooded, they are temporarily operating within the Public Education Center. The general affairs department has four sections: documentation, accounting, general services, and publicity. The relief department has four sections: investigation, fundraising, disaster relief, and reconstruction. Each section handles its respective tasks daily. Starting on the 9th, seven shelters were quickly set up to accommodate women, children, and disaster victims. (1) Zhengxin Girls' Middle School, sheltering women and children. (2) Peixin Middle School, sheltering those with families. (3) Paul Elementary School, sheltering elderly or disabled men. (4) South Gate Jesus Church, sheltering women and children. (5) East Station Jesus Church, sheltering women and children. (6) Xuzhou Civilian Residence, sheltering women and children. (7) Disability Center, sheltering women and children. Each shelter is assigned two managers. The number of disaster victims accommodated is temporarily limited to one thousand, for a period of half a month. Each man and woman receives one pound of steamed buns daily, and each child receives half a pound. The shelters are already overflowing. In addition to food for the people, the association is also working with the Red Swastika Society to sell grain at reasonable prices. The Red Swastika Society has already submitted a request through its Beijing office to the Ministry of Railways, which has approved the allocation of railcars to transport flour, 100 tons at a time, which should arrive in Xuzhou soon. Furthermore, representatives from various organizations, including Zhang Mingli, Liu Tianzhan, Lan Bohua, Li Fengru, Zhu Zhengxue, and Chen Suyi, have been sent to the provincial capital to request disaster relief funds. Regarding local transportation, the telegraph poles that were knocked down have been fully restored. When the water rose rapidly, Director Kuang moved one of the dynamos to a high point outside the city and rented houses in high places for the telegraph workers to ensure continued communication in case the water entered the city. Everything is now fully restored, and the lines are uninterrupted. The railway bridge ends at Liguo Post in North Xuzhou and Haozhai in West Xuzhou were excavated by farmers to release water, and have been repaired. Yesterday, the Longhai Railway bridge in Wayaodian, Xin'an Township, East Xuzhou, also had several sections of its foundation excavated by farmers. Railway personnel were dispatched to repair it, and it should be restored soon. However, to protect against possible breaches in the old Yellow River course, the city's residents are still divided into sections for defense. The entire city and its thirteen towns are divided into four zones to defend against breaches: (1) Hongfu Temple, defended by the towns of Pailou, Fuguozhen, and Tongyizhen. (2) Huisheng Temple, defended by the towns of Fushu, Zhongshan, Zhongshuzhen, and Datongzhen. (3) Outside the city, defended by the towns of Shishikou, Shaohuazhen, and Hepingzhen. (4) Outside the New East Gate, defended by the towns of Wentingzhen, Gongan, and Minshengzhen. (11th)

Emergency Relief Organized by Jiangsu Provincial Government

First Batch of Relief Funds: 39,000 Yuan

Distributed to Counties Along the Grand Canal and Those Severely Affected

This year, Jiangsu Province has suffered from prolonged rain, affecting 49 counties. The area north of the Yangtze River along the Grand Canal, located in the lower reaches of the Huai River, has been particularly devastated. Houses have been washed away, and residents are displaced. Although the Gaoyou Chelou Dam, Nanguan Dam, and Xinba Dam were all opened, the water level continues to rise relentlessly. This is truly a disaster unprecedented in decades. The Civil Affairs Department recently dispatched special commissioners to the affected counties to investigate the actual situation. They have been gone for many days. For the most severely affected counties, emergency relief should be promptly organized. Therefore, the department, in conjunction with the Agriculture Department, has drafted standard measures for organizing emergency relief and the allocation of relief funds, which have been submitted to the provincial government for approval. A sum of 39,000 yuan has been allocated for emergency relief. The details are listed below:

Amount of Relief Funds Allocated to Each County: Xinghua (most severe), 5,000 yuan; Liuhe (most severe), 5,000 yuan; Yancheng (severe), 4,000 yuan; Dongtai (severe), 4,000 yuan; Siyang (severe), 4,000

Page 12

yuan; Funing (still severe), 3,000 yuan; Taixian (less severe), 3,000 yuan; Gaoyou (less severe), 3,000 yuan; Tongshan (less severe), 3,000 yuan; Jiangpu (emergency relief), 5,000 yuan. All of the above funds have been claimed by the respective counties.

Standard Measures for Emergency Relief in Each County: (1) The county magistrate, in conjunction with the local relief branch, shall be responsible for organizing emergency relief in each county. (2) A detailed register of the poorest and next poorest households in the disaster area shall be prepared by the county in each district before the distribution of emergency relief. (3) When distributing emergency relief, the county magistrate and relief branch personnel shall personally visit the disaster area to verify and distribute relief according to the register of the poorest households. Relief for the next poorest households shall only be provided if there are surplus funds after relief has been distributed to the poorest households. (4) Three-part receipts shall be prepared for verification purposes during the distribution of emergency relief. The first part is the disaster victim's receipt, the second part is for reporting, and the third part is the stub. The provincial government may request the disaster victim's receipts and stubs from each county for verification if necessary. (5) Emergency relief shall be provided in the following four forms: 1. Distributing cash. 2. Distributing rations. 3. Establishing porridge kitchens. 4. Establishing shelters. (6) After completing emergency relief, each county shall prepare a list of relief funds and grain distributed in each district and township, along with a register of the four forms of relief and the reporting part of the three-part receipts, and submit them to the relevant department for verification.

Zhalan Coal Mine Budget Approved

130,000 Rubles Allocated for This Year's Restoration

The Dire State of the CER is Unprecedented

Harbin dispatch: Regarding the restoration of the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine, the board of directors instructed the railway bureau to prepare a budget. The budget was completed last month and submitted to the board. It was approved at an extraordinary meeting of the board of directors on August 5 and will be implemented immediately. A sum of 130,000 gold rubles has been allocated for construction costs this year, with a coal output of 20,000 tons, to be extracted using manual labor and open-pit mining. In subsequent years, the budget will be increased annually, with a maximum expenditure of 500,000 rubles per year. The amount of coal produced will also increase annually until the mine is restored to its original state. It has recently been announced that Hua, the deputy mine manager, has been replaced by Mao Yonggui, chief of the third section of the materials department of the railway bureau, who will soon go to the mine to recruit workers and begin mining. According to the Russian mine manager's suggestion, this year's mining will involve two steps: one, using new machinery to pump out the water near the mining area; and two, laying railway tracks in the mining area. These two tasks cannot be carried out simultaneously and must be separated by half a month. Therefore, the earliest date for coal production will be in late October. The business situation of the Chinese Eastern Railway (CER) has been gradually declining. The board of directors has reviewed the entire railway budget three times. After repeated reductions, it was finally finalized the other day, with expenditures estimated at 26 million gold rubles and revenues at 37.5 million gold rubles. However, the Russian side argued that the revenue estimate should be set at 32 million rubles, while the Chinese side argued that it could reach 37.5 million. Therefore, although this item has been approved by the board of directors, it still needs to be decided after Mordehui sends a telegram. Of the 37.5 million yuan in revenue, in addition to railway expenses, the following amounts are allocated to various agencies: (1) 132,000 rubles for the Superintendent's Office for the year; (2) 1.3 million rubles for the Railway Police Department for the year; (3) 600,000 Harbin dollars for the Governor's Office for the year; (4) 100,000 rubles for the Special District Court for the year; (5) 360,000 rubles for the Special Police Department for the year; (6) 200,000 rubles for the Railway Protection Army for the year; (7) 950,000 rubles for the Special Education Department; and 50,000 rubles for general expenses. If we add the losses from the exchange rate between rubles and Harbin dollars, the revenue is 40 million less than in 1925, the CER's most prosperous era. Expenditures have been reduced by 25 million. On August 1, the railway bureau decided on a new budget and announced the layoff of 317 employees, including more than 150 workers. The 36-shed railway sawmill had to be closed. The express passenger trains running between Harbin, Changchun, and Suifenhe have also been suspended. Since the first of this month, the Europe-Asia through train can no longer reach Harbin directly. This dire situation is unprecedented in the history of the CER. (8th)

Quick Dispatch from Wuhu

Continuous hurricanes have swept through here for three days non-stop. The floodwaters, stirred up by the wind, have posed an immense threat to the dikes which have miraculously remained intact. The Wanchun Dike, protecting the most fertile fields near Wuhu covering a total of one hundred thousand mu, was nearly breached the night before last. Fortunately, more than ten thousand workers managed to save it from disaster. However, many farmers have been forced to harvest their unripe rice, resulting in significant losses.

The Wuhu Flood Relief Association held a meeting today. Due to the high number of deaths among the disaster victims and the outbreak of epidemics, the association has established several Chinese and Western medical clinics in the city and countryside. In addition, organizations such as the Red Cross, Red Swastika Society, and Jisheng Hall have jointly formed burial teams.

Wang Leshan, brigade commander of the 171st Brigade of the 57th Division stationed in Wuhu, has noted that since the floods, bandits and disaster victims have been causing considerable disturbance in all directions, making local defense crucial. In addition to enforcing martial law and stationing troops at the electricity company and telephone bureau, Wang Leshan convened a public security meeting at the Red Swastika Society yesterday. The county magistrate, public security bureau chief, and chamber of commerce chairman were all in attendance. They decided on several measures to maintain local security and assigned responsibilities.

The bandit gangs in Liu'an, Anhui, have not yet been suppressed. Provincial Chairman Chen Diaoyuan had planned to travel from Anqing to Jiangxi today to meet with Chairman Chiang, intending to request that troops from Henan be dispatched to encircle and annihilate them. However, recent reports indicate a large number of bandit gangs in the Yingshan and Huoqiu areas. Chiang has ordered troops to be deployed to suppress them, so Chen has postponed his trip to Jiangxi.

The County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee has accused Zhu Dian, a gentry member from Wuhu, of local tyranny and has requested the county government to arrest him. Branch offices in various districts have also posted slogans demanding Zhu's execution for his disregard for the party and exploitation of farmers. (12th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Aircraft Crashes and Is Dismantled and Carried Away: Yesterday, an aircraft crashed in Xinqiao in the third district due to damaged parts. Farmers surrounded the aircraft and demanded compensation for the damaged crops. The issue was not immediately resolved. The pilot, with the aircraft protected by police dispatched from the branch office, felt safe and returned to Shanghai. The aircraft belongs to the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force. Today (13th), the pilot returned to Xinqiao and dismantled the aircraft, carrying the parts away. Regarding the farmers' demand for compensation, it is reported that they will be given 30 yuan as a gesture of goodwill.

High Court Sends Personnel to Investigate Prison: Due to the case of the death of prisoner Xu Qisheng by poisoning while in prison during the tenure of Zheng Ligeng, the former prison warden, the High Court has sent Yao Guozhang, director of the prison department, to Songjiang on the 12th to investigate. He is also tasked with facilitating the construction of a new prison and improving the living conditions of the prisoners.

Suzhou

Robbery with Injury in Xuzhuang Township: Yesterday (13th) at approximately 1:00 AM, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived at the home of Xu Ren'an, a farmer in Xuzhuang Township, Suzhou, in a boat. They broke down the door and entered, arbitrarily searching the house. They robbed silver dollars and clothing, as well as 15 shi of rice. As they left, they shot and injured Xu Ren'an and two others. The victim has reported the incident and requested a thorough investigation.

Dike Collapse in Hengjing Township Sweeps Away Farmers: Hengjing Township in Wuxian County, bordering Taihu Lake, is the lowest-lying area in the entire county. During this flood, eight out of ten parts of the fields in the township suffered total crop failure. Currently, the farmers in various villages are working hard to bail out water. However, the dike near Ducun Village in the township suddenly collapsed for more than ten zhang the other day. The water rushed in torrents, destroying many farmhouses. More than ten farmers were swept away by the waves and their whereabouts are unknown. In addition to ordering the farmers to work hard to repair the dike, the township office and public security bureau have reported the matter to the county government for instructions.

Change of President at Local Court: Ting Yaoting, president of the Wuxian County Local Court, has been ordered to be transferred to the Jiangning County Local Court as President. His vacant position will be filled by a Mr. Qu. Zhu is scheduled to depart for Nanjing on the 17th to take up his new post.

Wuxi

Wife and Concubine Lawsuit Incites Public Outrage: The death of Yu Ziming, a wealthy resident of Yangshuyuan in the 16th district of Xiyi, has sparked a lawsuit between his wife and concubine, which has not yet been resolved. It is reported that 34 people, including Yu Linzhang, Han Chu, and Zhang Boming, are outraged by this. Yesterday, they jointly filed a petition with the Wuxi County Court Procuratorate, stating that Yu's wife, Bian, has had an affair with Kuang Yunda for over a year, and that Kuang openly resides in her house. Everyone in the village knows about this. Yu's son, Yigen, has been ill for more than two years (suffering from a mild form of tuberculosis) and lives with his mother in Kuang's house, not returning to the Yu family. Everyone in the village knows this. On the afternoon of the 8th of this month, Bian returned home, and Xiao Yu Hu (Wen Zai's wife) asked her why Wen was not returning. Bian replied that he was doing well in the city. Seeing her strange expression, as if she was happy, Xiao Yu Hu said that since he was in litigation, the payment for the association fee was due, and asked her to pay it on his behalf. Upon hearing this, Bian raised her hand and slapped her face and went inside to get something, intending to leave. Da Yu Hu stopped her, causing a conflict between the two. Neighbors persuaded them to stop. Later, the village chief Qian Nianxiang went to a teahouse in the town to mediate the matter. As a result, both parties agreed not to press charges. At that time, none of them mentioned any poison. Later, Bian suddenly went back on her word and went to the city to press charges. Then, both Da Yu Hu and Xiao Yu Hu also went to the city to press charges. Bian suddenly presented longan pulp in court, claiming that it contained poison and that Da Yu Hu intended to poison her son Yigen. However, there are two points to this: 1. Yigen lives in Kuang's house and has not returned. 2. The village chief did not mention any poison during mediation. Moreover, Da Yu Hu's mother, Liu Yu, went to relatives' houses to attend a social gathering, and Wen Zai's concubine, Yu Hui, who is pregnant and about to give birth, lives separately two li away in Ge Lane. Bian's claims that they were all accomplices are clearly false accusations. Therefore, the villagers are presenting this public letter out of righteous indignation. They are all willing to testify in court.

Three Murders in One Day: Yesterday, there were three murder cases in one day. (1) At the home of Zhu A'gen, a villager in Xiadianqiao, 594, Jingyun City in the second district, Wang Wenkui, a Jingjiang native and cooper by trade, aged over fifty, hanged himself at 8:00 AM due to increasing living costs and severe financial difficulties. The chief of the county office reported the incident to the county court for an autopsy. (2) The County Court Procuratorate reported yesterday that it had received a report from Mao Jinji, chief of 17, that an unidentified male corpse had been found under the Huinong Bridge. Upon receiving the report, the Procuratorate sent Procurator Du and Shen, the coroner, to conduct an autopsy. The autopsy revealed that the corpse was about thirty years old, with a laceration on the left forehead. It appeared that the body had been moved. The chief was ordered to prepare a coffin and collect the body, pending further investigation. (3) Yesterday, while the Xiyi Yangxian steamship of the Gongyun Bridge Xi Yi Company was returning to Wuxi from Yi, it met the Xueyi ship on the way. A passenger on the Xue ship fell seriously ill. So, Fai Peichuan, the captain, talked to Wang Tingda, the tugboat owner of Yangxian, and transfered the sick passenger to the ship for treatment in Wuxi. Unexpectedly, when the ship arrived at the company's dock, the passenger had already died and could not be rescued. Yesterday the prosecutor's office was notified to inspect the body and prepare a coffin.

Zhenjiang

City's Rice Reserves Only Sufficient for One Month: Rice prices in this city are increasing daily. Although the Rice Industry Association has resolved that the price of Gaobai Tang rice should not exceed 15 yuan per shi, some are still selling it for 15.60 yuan. According to the Rice Industry Association's investigation, there are approximately 600,000 to 700,000 shi of rice in storage in this city, which can be milled into approximately 300,000 shi. The entire city consumes more than 1,000 shi of rice per day, which is only enough for one month. Furthermore, Anhui rice is banned from export, which will cut off the source of supply. The rice merchants have sent representatives to Shanghai to order a large quantity of foreign rice to be transported to Zhenjiang for supply.

Riverbank Collapse in Huangni Township: Due to rising tides, the riverbank in Huangni Township, Yonggu district of the first district, suddenly collapsed for more than twenty zhang the other day. All the dikes have become a watery expanse. Although no lives have been lost, the number of disaster victims is large. The river water east of Xiaoyi is now level with the riverbank, which is very dangerous. If it collapses again, thousands of households in the entire township will not escape disaster.

Nantong

Dredging Coastal Harbor Rivers: The harbor rivers such as Yaowang have become silted up. The eastern area had a big flood this year, which did not drain well. The county government is constructing a bureau to implement construction, resolving to dredge the port to provide work relief.

Civil Affairs Committee Reorganizing Warehouses: Shi Shuzhi, a member of the Civil Affairs Department, has been sent to Tongzhou to reorganize warehouses. The warehouses are currently being used by Tongzhong Shixiao, which will be negotiated to be recovered.

Investigating Theft of Jiang An Chart: The Jiang'an chart measured by the Nantong Baotu Association is stored in the Construction Bureau. The chart was stolen by the servant of former bureau director Yao Pengnian last November and sold to Shun Sheng Roasted Goods Shop near the Construction Bureau for 160 wen per catty. It has been recently discovered that many of the charts have been used as waste paper. The shopkeeper Wang Jinyu has been arrested by the Public Security Bureau, and the Construction Bureau has asked the court to investigate the matter.

Jiangyin

Rice Prices Soar Due to Shortages: The county has been affected by flooding, and there is also a shortage of supplies. Anhui rice, which was supposed to be available soon, has not arrived because the province has been severely affected by flooding. Rice prices have been soaring for days. White japonica rice has already reached 14 yuan and is expected to continue to rise. The Food Management Committee held a meeting on the morning of the 12th to discuss relief measures.

Education Bureau Requests Payment of 200,000 in Delinquent Treasury Bonds: The county government held a county political meeting on the 8th, presided over by County Magistrate Peng. He reported that Changshu Shazhou farmers had occupied the dry river in Fushou Township in the seventh district. He has sent a telegram to the county government to arrange a joint survey. The response telegram has been received, and officials from the Construction Bureau have been dispatched to conduct a survey. This government has dispatched Committee Member Xu Peidan to the countryside. He then discussed the Education Bureau's proposal to clear the outstanding treasury bonds, requesting the issuance of 200,000 yuan to comply with the original proposal. It was resolved that the proposal be approved, but 58,540 yuan from the Education Bureau's unpaid education expenses should be allocated to the Treasury Bond Fund Management Committee as collateral.

Zhang Chongzhi Reclaims House: Zhang Lin, Sha Zhixian, Zhang Chongzhi, Zhu Zhenyang, Shi Da, Wu Baolian, and others, the defendants in the Zhou Shuiping case, paid money to the provincial government to close the case and revoked the detention of property. After the disposition, the house of Zhang Chongzhi is being used by the County Party Headquarters. Zhang Chongzhi has submitted a request to the county to reclaim the house for living purposes. Yesterday (11th), Wang Shusheng of the County Party Headquarters spoke to the county government. Regarding the house issue, it can only be returned after a suitable address is found.

Difficult to Resolve Dam Opening: Due to the Changshu San'gan River dam blockage, the Sha people of Yangku Fushou Township in the seventh district have had their fields flooded and have requested the opening of the dam. After the county sent a telegram to the Changshu county government, it dispatched Construction Bureau Committee Member He and Jiangyin County Government Section Member Xu Peidan to conduct an inspection. The Sha people unanimously requested the opening of the dam, but the Changshu Sha people firmly refused. The situation has become a stalemate and there is still no solution. This matter needs to be handled by the superiors. Section Member Xu returned to the city to report on the evening of the 11th.

Gaoyou

Two Feet of Water Expected from Canal: The canal water level in this county has been gradually rising recently as water from the Yi River has arrived. Today (10th), the water level at the Imperial Wharf has reached 1 zhang 9 chi 3 cun and a half. According to canal officials, the Yi River suddenly rose 6 chi 5 cun on the 4th of this month, another 6 chi on the 5th, and another 5 chi on the 6th. In three days, the water rose 1 zhang 7 chi 5 cun, which should translate to a rise of more than 2 chi in the canal. The provincial government has received the telegram and has dispatched Sun Hongzhe, director of the Construction Department, to the post with 30,000 yuan. The funds will be handed to the Water Conservancy Bureau to quickly hire 1,000 workers to build canal embankments to prevent any unforeseen events. Director Sun is currently visiting Bao Ying, Huai'an, Huaiyin and other counties to inspect the dikes and water levels. The provincial government has also appointed He Haiqiao to visit the post to inspect the floods. It is reported that He will soon accompany County Magistrate Wang and Jiang Zhiqing of the Party Supervision Committee to Xinghua to inspect the disaster situation to facilitate relief efforts.

Yangzhou

Call to Protect Zhaoguan Dam: Recently, people up and down the river have been sending letters and telegrams on the issue of opening the Zhaoguan Dam, arguing for and against it. Li Mingyang, director of the Provincial Security Bureau, arrived in Yangzhou by special boat early on the 12th with Pei, chief engineer of the Water Conservancy Bureau, to inspect the water situation in northern Jiangsu and to inspect the possibility of opening the Zhaoguan Dam. The province also took the issue of Zhaoguan very seriously. The counties downstream such as Lvjiang and Jiangdu have sent multiple telegrams requesting the province to protect the dam. The general idea is that to open the dam and release water, the dike fields of the various salt reclamation companies should be sacrificed first to dredge the waterways. Otherwise, it will be difficult to open Zhaoguan. The water will stagnate downstream and will not be able to return to the sea, which will be harmful and not helpful. Yesterday (11th), the Shaobo Chamber of Commerce and Farmers' Association and the public sent a telegram to the Governor-General stating that the water volume in the counties east of the Shaobo Dike had exceeded 10 records, and the entire area was flooded. The disaster of the flooded tombs was severe. If the Zhaoguan Dam is opened again, it will put millions of lives in the counties down the river to death. They implore the Governor-General to order the protection of lives, so that the work of creation will be deep.

Northern Jiangsu, Where Riverbanks and Dikes are Simultaneously in Danger: This year's flood covers a wide area, and the Huai River basin is the most severely affected. The upper and lower reaches of the canal, four hundred or more li in length, are a vast expanse of water, which is very tragic. Due to the recent torrential rains in the Yi River, the water in the upper reaches of the canal has increased sharply, and the southeasterly wind has intensified, causing the tides to rush inland, putting the downstream areas in even greater danger than before the opening of the Chelou Dam, Nanguan Dam, and Xinba Dam. The riverbanks around Guazhou are also very dangerous. As of the evening of the 10th, two dikes had collapsed in Guazhou. Trees were being cut down day and night, and windows and walls were being dismantled to fill the dikes. (Guazhou and Shaobo are both in Jiangdu, Guazhou is south of the county seat, and Shaobo is north of the county seat.) On the 10th and 11th, due to the strong winds, the river tides and lake water (the west bank of Shaobo is Shaobo Lake) advanced fiercely at the same time, so that the dikes of the town were at a critical point. The Jiangdu Construction Bureau, under the order of the county magistrate, purchased 400 dan of Jiang firewood and transported it to the area this morning (12th) to raise the riverbanks to alleviate the immediate crisis.

Rugao

Northkan Changsha Pirates Active Again: Zhou Fuyu and other fishermen from Northkan, Juegang, witnessed five or six pirate ships chasing fishing boats in the Huangsha waters the other day. They opened fire and captured four fishing boats, including one belonging to the Cui family and one named Tuo Kaibang'er. They extorted a total of 24,000 yuan. The fishermen are crying out in pain as they open their mouths to the police. More than ten pirate ships have also been discovered near Changsha recently. They are demanding food and salaries from the residents along the coast. It was reported on the evening of the 5th that they had burned three fishing boats. Their momentum is very rampant.

Rice Prices Rise Sharply by More Than Two Yuan: Rice prices have recently risen sharply, from 12 yuan to more than 14 yuan per stone. It is said that there are few sources, and there is no hope for autumn harvests in the low-lying fields. It is expected that rice prices will continue to rise in the future.

Jiaxing

Arrest Warrant for Escaped Vagrants: The Jiaxing Vagrant Skills Training Center had eleven vagrants escape on the evening of the 8th at around 9 pm. Two individuals, Hong Jinkui and Wang Qifa, were subsequently apprehended and sent to the court for interrogation. The remaining nineteen fugitives, despite rigorous pursuit, have yet to be captured. Yesterday, the county government publicly announced the names, ages, and origins of those who escaped, and issued orders to the land and water military and police agencies to conduct a coordinated search.

Joint Trial of Bandits: After the looting in Puyuan Town, Jiaxing, many of the bandits have been apprehended and are being investigated according to the law. It is now known that detectives from the Third District of Jiangsu Water Police have also apprehended three bandits involved in the case, Liu Hesheng, Zhang Xueshun, and Wang Desan, in Shanghai. They were escorted to the Water Police District Headquarters, where, on the 12th, a joint trial was held by Zhou Weilie, the District Chief of the Water Police, Gong Shinong, the County Chief of Jiaxing, and Yang Xiuyan, the County Chief of Tongxiang. The suspect Zhang confessed that there were six boats involved in the looting of Puyuan, and Liu was a minor leader, with three boats under his command. However, despite rigorous interrogation, Liu and Wang have not revealed the truth. After the trial, the three suspects were taken back to Tongxiang by County Chief Yang for detention, and a telegram was sent to the provincial authorities for further instructions.

Pinghu

Execution of Mutinous Soldiers: The mutinous soldiers of the 16th Company, 4th Battalion, 7th Regiment of the Provincial Security Force, formerly stationed in Xincang, looted Xincang and Zhapu. Subsequently, seventy-two were arrested in Pinghu, Haiyan, and other places, and sent to the province for interrogation. Among them, sixty-five, including Jiang Jinhua, have been sentenced accordingly. However, the ringleaders, platoon leader Zhou Diyu (also known as Zhou Tingyu), squad leaders Wang Jinchu, Yang Yuqing, Ouyang Jin, Du Hairong (also known as Qian Lansheng), Zeng Yu, and Wang Maolin, the seventh person, were sentenced to death by the military court. After approval from the Provincial Government, they were escorted to the scene of the incident for execution. Yesterday, the 7th Regiment Commander, Shen Guocheng, led a platoon of soldiers under the command of the Special Service Company Commander, Chen Tianjing, escorted them to Pinghu on the Jiahe shift, and then transferred them to Xincang, where they were tied up at the Zhujia Alley execution ground and executed by firing squad one by one.

Xiaoshan

Kidnappers Confess to Detective Receiving Huge Bribe: The mother of Zhang Jiaxian, a resident of Changxiang, East Township, Xiaoshan, was kidnapped by bandits last year, demanding a ransom of 20,000 yuan. The family scraped together 19,500 yuan and entrusted Shen Baosheng, a fellow villager, to negotiate in Shanghai. Shen took advantage of the situation, resulting in insufficient ransom and the victim being killed. Upon learning of this, Zhang was overwhelmed with grief. Qian Asong, a bandit, has been captured by detective Chen Xijiu and sent to the Local Pacification Bureau for investigation. During yesterday's court interrogation, he confessed that Feng Binggang, the former detective captain, received a bribe of 300 yuan, and Shen Baosheng received 200 yuan. Arrest warrants have been issued for both of them, and they will be brought to justice for interrogation.

Shaoxing

Crackdown on Uncapitalized and Bogus Businesses: A man named Qiu Jichang in Doumen Town, Shaoxing, established a fake rice shop, Qiu Xiansheng Changji, without any capital, defrauding upstream suppliers of goods worth over 5,000 yuan, which he then sold and embezzled. After the creditor group obtained evidence, they filed civil and criminal lawsuits to investigate and prosecute him according to the law. They also posted a notice requesting the grain and rice trade association to forward a letter to the county chamber of commerce, urging them to take strict measures to crack down on uncapitalized and bogus businesses, maintain commercial ethics, and prevent small businesses from suffering endless harm.

Changxing

Lakeside Floods Await Urgent Relief: The northeast townships under the jurisdiction of Heping in Changxing, including Chengjing Village, which borders Wuxing, have approximately 2,000 households and about 42,000 mu of farmland. Since July 20th of the lunar calendar, there has been torrential rain for seven days and nights. On the 27th and 28th, violent storms and torrential rains added to the disaster, causing widespread flooding and cries of distress. All farming tools were swept away by the floodwaters, and houses and huts were completely washed away. The accumulated water has not yet receded, and people are living outdoors, exposed to the elements, without rice to cook, suffering from a severe calamity beyond words. They are now appealing to the authorities, hoping for urgent assistance.

Important News

The Eighth Annual Conference of the Chinese Economic Society

To be Held in Ningbo on September 1st

The Chinese Economic Society will hold its eighth annual conference in Ningbo this year. Because the Ningbo members of the society all work in Shanghai, the preparation has to be entrusted to local officials and gentry. Therefore, the president of the society, Ma Yinchu, went to Ningbo in mid-June to visit various sectors of the Ningbo Party, government, business, and academic communities, to discuss all the arrangements in person, which was warmly supported by all sectors. Consequently, a preparatory committee was organized, consisting of members of the society and local figures from the Party, government, business, and academic circles. Chen Baolin, the county chief of Yin County, was appointed as the vice chairman, responsible for carrying out the preparatory work. The conference is scheduled to be held from September 1st to September 6th. The venue will be in the Ningbo Chamber of Commerce, which has high buildings and a spacious hall, suitable for gatherings. The society has invited Cai Yuanpei to give a keynote speech, and has also accepted invitations from local groups to send members of the society to give lectures in various fields. At the same time, papers will be read at the conference. It is reported that the members who will be presenting papers have been specially selected by the Paper Committee organized by the head office, and they will be contributing excellent works to the society. As of today, there are more than 500 members of the society, and about 100 people are expected to attend. After the meeting, it is planned to visit famous scenic spots such as Putuo, Fenghua Xuedou, and Tiantong Yuwang. The preparatory committee has negotiated preferential arrangements with the Sanbei Ning Shao Merchants and Sanbei Company. Members attending the meeting who travel to Ningbo by sea can collect vouchers from Li Gufan at Yuehua Middle Business Company, No. 36 Edward Road, Shanghai, before the 26th of this month. With this voucher, they can exchange for half-price tickets from the company, applicable to both the deluxe and standard cabins. Those traveling from Beijing, Tianjin, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Wuxi, and other places should also collect vouchers from Zhu Binyuan at the Economic Committee of the Nanjing Legislative Yuan, and exchange them for half-price tickets from the Railway Bureau. The guidebook for the eighth annual conference of the society has been printed by the preparatory committee and distributed to the members. According to the schedule, members need to stay overnight in Tiantong and Putuo. If they are concerned about the cleanliness of the bedding in the temples, it is best to bring one or two sheets. It is reported that the cost of the conference is calculated based on 100 people. The ships, sedan chairs, and hotel rooms for visiting scenic spots must be prepared in advance by the preparatory committee. Therefore, members attending the meeting must notify Chen Baolin of the Yin County Government a few days before the meeting so that he can prepare everything on their behalf.

Biologist

Zhang Zuoren Publishes Research Results in France

The annual meeting of the Belgian National Academy of Sciences opened in mid-July this year. The Chinese biologist Mr. Zhang Zuoren took this opportunity to announce the results of his research over the years: (1) the effect of different culture mediums on the inheritance of trichomonas; (2) the effect of different bacteria in the culture medium on the inheritance of trichomonas; (3) the effect of different PH components in the culture medium on the inheritance of trichomonas; (4) the evolution of large and small nuclei during the division of multinucleated trichomonas. Among them, the third item is a completely new research, which can be said to be a new path in biology. Therefore, it aroused the deep interest of the scholars present and won highly honorable praise.

Registration Begins for the National Mandarin Discussion Conference

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association is convening the National Mandarin Discussion Conference and the 20th Annual Members' Meeting, scheduled to open at 8:30 AM on August 16th at the New World Nan Huang Palace Theater on Xizang Road in Shanghai. In addition to the announcements that have already been made, the representatives who have registered include Chen Jianheng from the Shandong Education Department, Li Zhengkai from the Jiangxi Education Department, and Han Shoujin from the Jiangsu Education Department. The motions submitted by the Education Departments include: (1) Elementary school textbooks should uniformly use phonetic symbols for annotation; (2) Provinces and cities should quickly establish phonetic symbol training programs; (3) Compile a standard Mandarin dictionary (submitted by the Anhui Education Department); (4) Provinces, cities, and counties should actively promote Mandarin education (submitted by the Jiangxi Education Department); (5) Vigorously promote document reform and effectively promote Mandarin (submitted by the Shandong Education Department). It is also reported that the association is scheduled to start registration at 2:00 PM today at the association's office in Pingle Lane on Xizang Road.

Soochow

Law School Adds Graduate Institute

The Soochow Law School on Kunshan Road in Shanghai has long been known for its efforts in cultivating legal professionals. It has recently been announced that, starting next semester, the school will add a graduate institute to provide law scholars with opportunities for further study. Admission will be limited to graduates of university law departments. The program will last for two years, with the first year dedicated to coursework and the second year dedicated to writing a thesis. Graduates who meet the requirements will be awarded a Master of Laws degree. As for the curriculum, the main focus of this session will be the comparative law of various countries, with particular emphasis on English and American civil law, French civil law, German civil law, Japanese civil law, Soviet Russian civil law, and Chinese civil law. The professors hired, such as Wu Jingxiong, Sa Laide, Yao Qiyin, Liang Renjie, Liu Shifang, Zhang Zhirang, and Dai Xiuzan, are all well-known figures in the legal field. It is also reported that classes will be held from 6:00 PM to 8:00 PM from Monday to Friday, which is very convenient for those who have jobs during the day but are interested in studying law in depth. It is also reported that the number of students for this academic year is temporarily limited, so those who wish to apply should do so as soon as possible. The application period is from August 20th to September 10th. The school also has a brochure available for reference.

Pan Gongzhan Lectures at Nanyang Summer School

Mr. Pan Gongzhan, the director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and a representative of Shanghai at the National Assembly, gave a lecture at the Overseas Chinese Memorial Hall of the Nanyang Commercial Senior High School Summer School on Tongji Road at 10:00 AM today (the 13th). More than 300 teachers and students from the school attended. The topic was originally set to be labor issues, but temporarily changed to the knowledge that students should have, because most of the listeners were young students from the summer school. He said that everyone should be responsible for transforming society, and students are no exception. Therefore, the purpose of studying now is different from before. For example, learning English was previously only for the purpose of becoming a comprador, translator, or other comprador-like job. Now, it is to use English to study advanced academic knowledge, use the material civilization of Europe and the West to improve China's weaknesses, and promote the progress of the general society. Finally, he instructed that whether studying or doing things, one should think far and work hard near, and the wording was vivid and the voice was clear and bright. The lecture lasted for an hour and a half, and the listeners applauded and cheered at every insightful point.

Mr. Niu Yongjian of Shanghai, in view of China's backward production, the people's livelihood is declining, the lack of gardens everywhere, and the dilapidated appearance of villages and towns, contacted local enthusiastic people to establish the Qiangshu Horticulture School in his hometown (Maqiao Township) in the summer of the first semester of the 19th year to take the lead in the national trend, and invited Guo Houan, the director of the Capital Park and a professor at Central University, to serve as the principal. In the past year, internal planning has been carried out with all efforts. Chinese Student Tennis Doubles Final

Qian and Guo Win the Championship

Defeating Yu Tianguang and Feng Nianci 3 to 1

1-6, 6-3, 8-6, 6-4 丨

The Shanghai Chinese Student Tennis Doubles Final was held at the Chinese Tennis Court at 5 PM yesterday. Qian Yaobin and Guo Yujie won the championship by defeating Yu Tianguang and Feng Nianci 1-6, 6-3, 8-6, 6-4. Qian and Guo are both rising stars. Qian's forehand and backhand strokes and overhead smashes all show skill, and Guo's net play also made many contributions. Yu Tianguang was the champion of the Shanghai Group B tournament last year, and his tennis skills have long been well-known. However, he was not in good spirits yesterday and lacked strength. In addition, Feng Nianci's tennis skills were relatively poor, and the two could not cooperate, which led to their defeat.

Qian Yaobin and Guo Yujie (1丨6 6丨3 8丨6 6丨4) Yu Tianguang and Feng Nianci

Amazing Start

After the start, Yu and Feng were quite successful, winning the first game with a score of 6-1. Qian and Guo tried their best to struggle, but because they lost too much, it was difficult to recover. Yu and Feng won with a score of 6 to 1.

Taking Advantage of the Opportunity

Starting from the second set, Qian's group took the advantage, and the weaknesses of Yu's group were exposed. One was careless, and the other could not connect, so that the enemy could easily advance. Although they formed a situation of 3 to 2, they were eventually defeated by Qian and Guo with a score of 6 to 3.

Almost Succeeded

In the third set, the situation was the most even. Yu and Feng had many opportunities to win, and they had an advantage of 6 to 5. In the next game, Yu's group took the lead with a score of 3 to 2. If they could win another game, they could win back this set. At this critical moment, Yu's group could not win in one go, but lost three consecutive games. It was a pity that they failed. Qian and Guo won with a score of 8 to 6, creating an excellent situation.

Remaining Power Concludes Victory

In the fourth set, Yu and Feng shook off their spirits and tried to recover. At first, they had a great advantage, but eventually Feng Nianci lost points repeatedly, and Yu Tianguang was also weaker at this time. Qian and Guo took advantage of the victory and completed the victory in one go, capturing the whole work with a score of 6 to 3.

Today's Singles Order

丨Starting at 3:15 PM丨

Guo Pengnian vs Ma Anquan

Qian Yaobin vs Chen Chuanzhang

Record of the Yoyo Cup Singles Tennis Match

Yesterday, a total of three matches were played. The Guo-Tu group's combat power was the strongest. Guo won over Tu with a score of two to one. In the first game of the first set, after each hitting fourteen shots, Guo won two consecutive points, taking the first game. Tu won the second game with a serve. Both sides had their own strengths in rallies. Zheng won the first set with a score of six to two. The competition in the second set was fierce. Guo initially won three consecutive games, but Tu refused to be weak and reversed the situation, winning four to three over Guo. Tu lost the seventh and eighth games consecutively due to errors, and then tied the score at five to five. Guo then won two consecutive games, thus winning the second set. In the final set, Tu used his cannonball serve and net play to win three consecutive games. Guo then defended cautiously, and at five to four, Tu still won the final set with a serve. Overall, both players had their own strengths in their skills, and the victory or defeat was in the hands of the goddess of luck. The results of each group are as follows:

Departing at 7 o'clock on the 16th

Changes in Transportation Costs

Because there are many passengers on the Beijing-Shanghai line, it is stipulated that discounts cannot be granted on Sundays and public holidays, and there has been a slight change in the transportation cost, which is now changed to one dollar and fifty cents. Registration closes today at 4 o'clock at China Products Company, No. 141 Guizhou Road.
