Free Talk

World Anecdotes

— Hai Ke

The Strongman in Prison

In Blackpool, England, a man was jailed for a crime and sentenced to six months' imprisonment. His hands were shackled and tied behind his back, making it virtually impossible to use any force. Who knew that he would break the shackles, attack the patrolmen, and even smash the iron bars in the cell into pieces? With such divine power, he can be called the second Samson.

A Chapel Made of Cardboard

Twenty miles outside Johannesburg, the first town in Transval, Africa, on the border of Benoni, there is a chapel made entirely of cardboard, without a single piece of wood. It was transported from England piece by piece twenty-one years ago and assembled locally. Although it has been a long time, it is still usable. It was recently moved from Benoni to another location and will probably be usable for many more years.

Dreaming of a Thief

Walter Baker, the manager of a safe manufacturing factory in Wolverhampton, England, was sleeping at home one night when he dreamed that something unexpected had happened at the factory. After waking up in shock, he rushed to the factory and caught three young thieves who had already broken in.

Talking about Qingcheng in the Dog Days

— Zhang Yan

The place where Wu Peifu is currently visiting

This newspaper's Chengdu dispatch on the 7th stated that Wu Peifu had arrived in Chengdu and was staying at Zhaojue Temple, and that he was going to Qingcheng Mountain in Guan County for sightseeing. When I visited Chengdu in the past, I visited Qingcheng once. The mountains and rivers there are no less beautiful than West Lake. Based on what I know, I will record one or two things for the readers.

Zhaojue Temple: The temple is located two or three miles outside the north gate of Chengdu and is the most famous large monastery in the county. There are many monks and the temple property is wealthy. The temple site is chair-shaped, with ancient trees towering on all sides and beautiful scenery. The halls and buildings are majestic, with carved beams and painted pillars. During the Qing Dynasty, it had more than 7,000 mu of farmland, half of which was confiscated by Zhou Xiaohuai, the patrolling police officer. Now there are only two or three thousand mu of farmland, which is still a huge monastery. Therefore, it is a place for celebrities to stay.

Guan County's Special Weather: Guan County is located in the western part of Chengdu, about one hundred miles away from the province. The folk customs are simple and honest. The main products are medicinal materials and wool. Half of the city wall is靠山. The climate is suitable for all seasons. The most amazing thing is that the men, women, old and young in the county, even without Zhuge Liang's ability to calculate, can know the future weather. Determine whether the next day will be sunny, cloudy, windy, or rainy. The method is after every day is over. If there is a strong wind, the next day will be calm and the sun will fill the window. If there is no wind, the next day will be either rainy or cloudy. The locals have tried it hundreds of times without fail. It is truly an amazing thing.

Qingcheng Mountain's Beautiful Scenery: Qingcheng Mountain is about fifty miles away from Guan County. The mountain has thirty-six peaks, each with its own scenery. There is no winter or summer. The climate is suitable. Therefore, the Sichuan people have the saying that the scenery of Qingcheng Mountain covers the world. Every summer, the盛况 of Chinese and foreign people who go there to escape the heat is no less than Mogan or Lushan. The mountain stone is engraved with the words "The First Peak in the World." The characters are very large and powerful. Written by Huang Yunhu, the Qing Chengdu prefect. There is the Shangqing Palace in the mountain. Chunyang 覯. Heavenly Master along the temples. The mountain scenery includes Mandarin Duck Well. Its water is clear and sweet. When brewing tea, even the water from Tiger Spring is inferior. There is also Golden Whip Rock. A black tiger and Xuan Tan Zhao Gongming's golden whip are hanging between the cliffs. When the sun rises, it reflects with the red sun. The Xia light is brilliant. The sting is dazzling. It is a spectacle. The rest of the beautiful scenery cannot be recorded. I will摘 its big ones. Slightly recorded one or two.

Gold Plate and Silver Cup

— Zheng Yimei

Gold plate and silver cup. It is also the name of a medicine. However, it is not something that can be bought from ordinary pharmacies. It is a rare treasure if it is obtained by chance. I heard a guest talk about it yesterday. It's very novel and pleasing. The guest is from Puqi. There is a scholar in his place who is known for his romantic 放诞. He spends his days indulging in fine wine and women. Eventually, he develops a numb paralysis. Acupuncture and massage are ineffective. He stays in a room, unable to step out of his bounds. His heart is very worried. This goes on for three years. One day, a Sichuan monk comes. His beard and face are pale. His tattered robe reveals his elbows. He says he can cure intractable diseases and strange ailments. The scholar knows of this. Because the doctors are helpless, he summons the monk to try. The monk takes one look and gives him a pinch of powder to swallow. He also prepares six small bags for him to take without fail during his coming recovery. Seven days later, the monk comes uninvited. The scholar is already completely healed. He stands up and expresses his gratitude. He asks the monk by what technique he achieved this. The monk replies, "This is the national treasure of the gold plate and silver cup. This old monk dares not take the credit." Then he describes the origin of the gold plate and silver cup. Last year, while traveling to Hubei, he stayed at a temple. The temple is near a field. In the twilight dusk, a shepherd boy led his calf past. I have always liked to listen to the innocent words of shepherd children. The children all consider me to be 親. One day, someone saw a dog leaving excrement on cow dung, which piled up into a small hill. It was quite interesting. I was very happy when I heard this, saying, "This is a good medicine that I have been seeking for years but have not been able to obtain." He ordered the child to lead him to the place. He found it,裏ed it, and returned. It was dried, exposed to the sun, and ground into powder. This is the so-called gold plate and silver cup. However, you must not let the sick family know about it first. If they know, they will definitely vomit and not accept it. The medicine will not reach the inner organs. The reason why I did not tell you in advance is precisely because of this." After the scholar recovered from his long illness, he gave the monk a lot of money as a reward. The monk did not accept it, saying, "There is no need for this thing." He is also a great monk. According to the Yunlu Man Chao, water lilies are gold cups and silver platforms. Now, according to what the Sichuan monk said, I don't know if there is this name in ancient medical books. I also ask the medical experts of today.

Water Mirror

— Yi Si

Farmers in Jiujiang Town, Nanhai County, Guangdong Province, mostly engage in fish farming. People in this profession possess an extraordinary technique for assessing water levels. Each year, on the day of the Beginning of Spring, those skilled in this art go to the riverbank and draw water into an earthenware bowl. By merely using their fingers to measure its weight, they can determine the height of the water rise for that year and whether there will be floods. This has been proven accurate repeatedly and is truly a remarkable skill.

Furthermore, by observing where cicada shells adhere between spring and winter, and the distance from the ground, one can also predict the depth of the water rise for that year. Unfortunately, they only know how to do it but cannot explain the reason behind it. Hopefully, scientists will pay attention to this.

A Gramophone Summer Solace

— Gu Yan

The blazing sun makes one feel as if sitting in a furnace. How can one escape such intense heat? To seek physical and mental pleasure, one must find alternative paths to enjoyment. I borrowed a set of the latest records from the Beka company from a friend. There were about thirty types. I listened to each one carefully and didn’t feel bored even after three days and nights. They were truly captivating. Now, I will offer my humble opinions and record them. Ma Lianliang’s "Beheading the Son" creates a unique style in its aria. Liu Bo can no longer claim exclusive excellence. "Beating the Nephew at the Grave" is distinguished by its recitative. Wang Shaolou’s "Lamenting at Changban Slope in the Fifth Watch" is clear, melodious, and uniquely original. Bao Lian Deng's old-style "erhuang" quick "sansanyan" style is unrestrained and directly approaches Shu Yan. His duet with Shang Xiaoyun in "Qiu Hu Teasing His Wife" is excellent in both singing and delivery. Yan Jupeng’s "Zhu Lian Village" has a voice like metal and stone, showing considerable skill. Tan Xiaopei and Luo Wenkui’s "Selling the Horse" features close and seamless dialogue. Shang Xiaoyun's "Teaching the Son" has a beautiful voice that is naturally endowed, making her excel in her field. "Xiangsi Village Persuading Farming" presents new arias in succession, flowing and pleasing to the ear. Xue Yanqin and Tan Fuying’s duet in "Visiting the Mother in the Palace" shows Xue excelling in sweetness and charm, while Tan is distinguished by his aged voice. It can be said that both are beautiful. Xue Yanqin and Xiao Changhua’s "Su San Escorted Under Guard" features one with flavorful melodies and the other with authentic Beijing dialect. Du Liyun’s "Hibiscus Sword" and Yu Shuang’s "Scolding the Palace" can be said to achieve the same result through different paths. The quick "sansanyan" style in "Yu Tang Chun Visiting the Prison" has never been seen on records before. Liyun’s unconventional approach is also novel and appealing. Jin Shaoshan and Ma Fulu’s duet in "Fa Men Temple" and "Investigating the Underworld" feature both singing and dialogue that are majestic and decisive. In terms of structure, it has reached the pinnacle. Li Duokui’s "Ganlu Temple" and "Beheading the Son" capture the essence of Gong. Drum King Liu Baoquan’s two pieces "Bowang Slope" and "Xu Mother Scolds Cao" have a generous style and full energy. Bai Yunpeng’s "Daiyu Returns to Heaven" and "White Emperor City" are both graceful and majestic. Lao Wagua’s "Awakening Golden Bell" and Zhang Ye’er’s "Four Teachings Song" are full of humor and vividly expressive. They are worthy of the title of the two great comedians of the North and South. Other pieces include Wang Caiyun's ditties, Shen Jian’an and Xue Xiaoqing’s "Pearl Pagoda," Liu Cuixia, Li Yufen and Wen Jinfang’s "B繃調," Ms. Hu Zhou Shuan and Ms. Bao Yongzhen's new-style songs, German military drills, Russian boatmen's songs, etc. The singers put their whole spirit into it, and the recording is clear and accurate, making them all beautiful and pleasing to the ear, catering to the preferences of record fans.

Art World News (1) Jiangdu Zhou Wufang excels at skin carving and using bamboo fan bones, preserving the bamboo surface and creating landscape, figure, and flower paintings with green reeds. The brushstrokes, composition, and carving are all wondrous, like painting. He also expertly carves small ivory pieces, Buddha statues, and nudes. He is currently residing in the Dadong Apartment on Malan Road. Price lists are available upon request. Also, He Qiyu is skilled in calligraphy and painting and excels at shallowly carving fan bones. Each fan with both sides and the bone carved costs only eleven yuan. Qinghua Bookstore on Jiaotong Road is the general agent for receiving orders. (She)

Art World News (2) Jinling female painter Chen Yufeng is skilled in poetry and excels in painting. Her brushwork is divine, following the style of the Song and Yuan dynasties. This time, she came to Shanghai and, at the request of various circles, specially presented five hundred fan surfaces, which were fully reserved in an instant. However, various circles have sent letters requesting an extension. Therefore, she is specially offering another fifty pages for one week only. Each page still costs two yuan for ink fee. Regular paintings are four yuan per foot. Screens are half price. The receiving address is Nanyang Socks Factory (Jin Binglan) on Nanjing Road.

Travels in India (80)

— Ling Hua

Since yesterday, the newspapers have reported that Gandhi and the government have reached an understanding and will cease all non-cooperation movements. The government's condition is to convene a national conference. I asked someone about this matter: Can Gandhi actually cancel the various movements? The person said that this is Gandhi's strategy, taking a temporary break to convene a national conference for a grand promotion. If the conference is not to his liking at that time, he will break again, and their collective strength will be greater. Gandhi has spent much of his life in prison, once for six years and once for four years, a total of five or six times. It is no wonder that he has no smile on his face and often cries. Gandhi's revolution is an inward revolution. Alas, it can be said to be difficult. Whether it will succeed, I do not know. Yesterday, monks gave lectures and reports on the situation of physical beauty, mentioning Gandhi's name more than ten times in one session. It can be said that the entire Indian nation thinks of Gandhi like the Chinese think of Amitabha Buddha.

Confucius once said, "Is man really inferior to birds?" It is easier to be a bird than to be a man. The great difference between the Indian and Islamic religions is that Islam forbids eating pork, while India forbids eating beef. Both are forbidden items. However, in the year 743 AD, there was an Islamic king named Walid II, who scorned the Quran, openly ate pork, drank alcohol, and did not pray. In that same year, an Indian religious saint named Guru Nanak Saheb created a new sect, harmonizing Islam and India, gathering people from both religions to form a new sect. There were charitable people in Islam who also agreed with his prohibition of eating beef and inclined towards him. Later, his disciples gained considerable influence and clashed with the [other] sect, resulting in many mutual killings. Even today, there are still 70,000 followers, forming a new sect. When they fought each other, the Indians also deliberately used pig bones to resist them. One pig and one cow have become major problems in West and Central Asia and India. It is like the Manchus entering the customs, causing countless deaths because of a single queue [hairstyle]. In the religious wars of the Middle Ages, countless people were killed because of a single idol. Now, Marx wants to solve it with a single materialistic history, but it seems not easy. If you live among Indians and Muslims for a long time, you will know that many problems are mostly due to the differences in religious habits, beliefs, and customs, and are not material problems. Even the prohibitions on pork and beef have nothing to do with material things. What can be done about it? If it were in Egypt, cats would also become a major problem because ancient Egypt had a punishment for killing cats. The punishment was very severe, almost equal to killing a person. It is not easy to be a human being in different customs in different places.

Rotary Club Talking

Woman, Woman (19)

— Yao Su Feng

When Xiao Rong’s wife heard that they had already returned to Shanghai, she felt very sad, but there was nothing she could do, so she reluctantly went home. How would she know that Xiao Rong had only moved to another hotel?

When she returned home, the more she thought about it, the more uneasy she became, and the more she worried. She felt that she had to find Xiao Rong and ask him herself. Therefore, she came up with a plan and decided to go by herself. At that time, she discussed it with her father-in-law and mother-in-law, and everyone thought this method was good. So, after she inquired about and firmly remembered the address of the school where Xiao Rong was studying, she took some travel expenses and rushed to Shanghai alone, regardless of everything.

On this day, Xiao Rong had been accompanying Miss Ding in Suzhou for two days and was a bit tired of playing. Moreover, Xiao Rong was often worried that perhaps more unfortunate things would find him, so he told Miss Ding that he wanted to return to Shanghai. Miss Ding did not object.

After Xiao Rong’s wife arrived in Shanghai, she hired a rickshaw and went straight to Xiao Rong’s school according to the address she had remembered. She asked the doorman, "Is there a student here named Lu Rongqing from Suzhou?"

"Lu Rongqing! Yes, there is! He is not in school now!" The doorman looked at the sign hanging on the wall and answered like this.

"Then where did he go? Will he come back tonight?" She asked again.

"That, I don't know!"

She had no choice but to sit and wait at the school gate. Her only hope was that she could meet Xiao Rong when he returned to school. But one hour, two hours passed, and it was already eight o'clock in the evening, and she was still disappointed. However, she still patiently waited without leaving. The doorman also felt surprised and asked her, "Do you have any urgent business with Lu Rongqing? You can just tell me, and I can pass it on to him. If you keep waiting for him, you might not see him for days! Because it’s summer vacation now."

She still did not leave, thinking about her own future, she could not help but shed a few tears in secret. It was not until ten o'clock when the school gate was about to close that she had no other way to stay here, so she had to leave disappointed and find a small hotel to stay nearby.

She could not sleep all night and cried several times. As soon as it dawned, she immediately rushed to Xiao Rong’s school.

"Has Lu Rongqing returned?" she asked.

"No!" the doorman replied in surprise. So, she still sat on the chair at the school gate and waited.

Many students who were going in and out saw such a sad-faced woman sitting at the school gate, and everyone began to inquire about it. It happened that Li Wenyao came to the school that day, and everyone talked about this matter.

Calm Seas for Bullion Trading

Fluctuating within the 75 Taels Mark Yesterday, the 13th, the bullion market seemed to be softening, but the seas were calm, fluctuating within 775 taels. The overall market difference was only a few taels. As a result, there was a slight drop. The trading volume among dealers was mixed, but there were no large transactions. Although the silver price rose, it withered as soon as it opened. The foreign exchange market was quite stable, with a slight upward trend in the future. The market was even more sluggish, with fluctuations of only one or two taels. As the settlement date approaches, many parties are still willing to post [margin].

Opening Slightly Lower The September contract opened slightly lower in the morning, down 2.2 taels, at 771.5 taels. The spot market remained unchanged. The silver price rose by one-eighth in both public and private telegrams. Although US stocks fell, it did not cause any movement. Next, it was 1.2 taels. Wanxing Shunli Goods and other firms took the lead in selling. Soon, Tong Taichang Zhifeng Yong and others bought in, immediately raising the price by 3 taels to 74.5 taels. Zhifeng Yong Yuanmao Yong and other arbitrageurs bought in, so it rose again, reaching 75 taels at 9:50. Extremely Stagnant Securities and Bond Market

Slightly Smaller Transaction Volume Compared to Previous Day, Exceeding 10.7 Million

Yesterday, the spot bond market was extremely sluggish, with no transactions all day. The futures market was also very calm. Except for the unified tax transactions, which were not too quiet, the others were far from the previous level. The total was only more than 10.7 million yuan. Major investors were watching, and the market was very quiet. The prices only hovered around two or three jiao all day. Except for the demobilization bonds and the 20 [year] customs bonds expiring in August, which were down by a little more than half a yuan, the others only fell by one or two jiao.

Cotton Yarn and Cotton Flower Market Trends Diverge

The yarn market rose in the afternoon after falling in the morning. The trend remained chaotic, and the changes were quite rapid. However, the price of American cotton continued to fall slightly, so there were still many sellers. In the afternoon, it was reported that the US Department of Agriculture would abandon collecting one-third of the US cotton crop. As a result, market sentiment was greatly shaken, and the situation changed abruptly. The buying interest was tense, and the prices for all months jumped by more than two taels. Later, a major player sold, and the closing price slightly recovered. Most people predicted that the price of American cotton might rise again, so the market atmosphere was very tight. The Rongxing Company continued to buy and increase its position, and the amount was still huge. However, the actual situation was not good.

People's Standard Cotton Fell in Morning and Rose in Afternoon The People's Standard Cotton market opened in the previous session. Due to the poor condition of American cotton, the market was very weak, and the prices fell by 5.6 qian to 2.47 qian. In the afternoon, the price of American cotton rose sharply by more than two taels due to news. Later, due to pressure from major players, it fell by a few qian. The transaction volume was 88,350 bales. It was found that Gongtai sold 1,200 bales, Ruidai 4,200 bales, Dafu 2,000 bales, Gengfeng 2,650 bales, Yiyu 1,550 bales, Xinhua 1,400 bales, and Xincheng 4,150 bales. Jifeng bought 1,500 bales, Rongxing 4,700 bales, Yichang 3,050 bales, Dachang 2,350 bales, Changfeng 1,000 bales, and Meiji 1,200 bales. The closing prices are recorded on the left.

More Than 1,000 Bales of Spot Cotton The sales of spot yarn were flat. It was found that the statistics of various groups buying throughout the day totaled more than 1,000 bales. Fellow traders entered 460 bales, Yunnan entered 385 bales, Sichuan entered 175 bales, the hinterland entered 100 bales, Guangdong entered 100 bales, the Northern Gang entered 45 bales, and Jiangxi entered 35 bales.

Cotton Market Improves in the Afternoon

The cotton market initially declined then improved, but foreign cotton remained sluggish, and gold prices softened. Moreover, overseas surpluses caused unease, leading to a hesitant sentiment. However, in the afternoon, news from the U.S. Agricultural Administration suggested a one-third reduction in U.S. cotton production. Whether this proposal will materialize remains uncertain. Market sentiment tightened sharply, and buying interest surged, causing prices to soar by five or six cash. However, major players continued to sell, indicating a lack of confidence in the cotton market's future.

Hankow Standard Benefits from U.S. Cotton News. The opening price for Hankow Standard was down four, eight, and five cash due to the continued weakness in the global cotton market and hesitant sentiment. In the afternoon, driven by the U.S. cotton news, prices surged by four, five, and six cash. Total transactions amounted to 211,900 bales. Sales included Hengda (4,000 bales), Tianlong (3,700 bales), Ruida (9,500 bales), Xincheng (8,200 bales), Yuanda (3,400 bales), and Xiesheng (2,200 bales). Purchases included Heshen (5,000 bales), Gengfeng (8,500 bales), Xincheng (3,300 bales), Xinheng (4,400 bales), Zhenda (3,900 bales), Dachang (4,100 bales), Dachangcheng (3,200 bales), and Dafeng (3,100 bales). Proposal to Destroy One-Third of U.S. Cotton

Washington, 12th. The Department of Agriculture sent letters to the governors of the 14 cotton-growing states, proposing to destroy one-third of the new cotton crop. If the states can assist in implementing this, the U.S. government will withhold its 1.3 million bales of stored cotton from the market in the following year. According to the government's estimate on August 8, cotton production will reach (15,584,000 bales). The carryover at the end of July was (9,130,000 bales), and the government-stored cotton was (1,300,000 bales), totaling (26,014,000 bales). If one-third of the new cotton crop can be destroyed and the Department of Agriculture withholds its stored cotton, the U.S. cotton supply would be approximately (19,500,000 bales).

Additionally, if ten major states accept the proposal to destroy one-third of U.S. cotton, it may be implemented.

Rice Market in Zhabei Plunges by One Yuan

The Nanshi Market Temporarily Stabilizes

Nanshi: Supplies from various groups remained limited due to morning wind resistance. Supplies only started arriving around 10:00 AM, including shipments from Tonglibei, Lili Liantang No. 4, and Nangang No. 3 and 4, Pinghu No. 22 and 23. Limited volume was traded. Special Chang Geng opened at 18.9 yuan, with other grades priced accordingly. Although the supply of foreign rice was not large, the demand from customers and local merchants seemed deterred by the high prices, leading to a slight softening. The market appeared weak.

Zhabei: The supply from the west road remained strong, but trading in the local market became increasingly sluggish. Although nearly a thousand piculs of Bo Dao and Early Rice were offered, prices plunged by about one yuan. Su Chang Bai Geng and Kunshan rice each fell by 7 or 8 jiao. There was little interest in Lu Yang Jian and Bu Jian. The downstream outlook was weak. Limited quantities of glutinous rice arrived. Although liquor merchants were interested, local sales were not strong. The market opened half a yuan lower. Nearly one hundred piculs of new Geng arrived, jointly purchased by Yuchen Tai and Hesheng, but no transactions were completed.

Sugar Market: Dutch Red Sugar Continues to Offer Over 2,000 Bags

Yesterday's telegrams from sugar-producing areas indicated that the price of Cuban spot sugar remained unchanged. New York sugar futures for December fell by one point, while May futures for next year rose by one point. Other months showed no changes. Java spot sugar also remained unchanged. There were few transactions in the public market due to sluggish sales, but sentiment remained firm. Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse granulated white new goods were priced at 11 taels and 5.5 qian, No. 20 medium granulated white at 11 taels and 0.05 qian, finely ground granulated white at 11 taels and 6.5 qian, Dutch red sugar No. 8/9 at 9 taels and 4 qian, bowl blue at 8 taels and 7.5 qian. Taikoo sugar B was priced at 12 taels and 1 qian, CW at 11 taels and 9 qian, DY at 11 taels and 9.5 qian, HM at 11 taels and 4.5 qian, and HX at 11 taels and 8.5 qian. Transactions were scarce, and the market remained flat. Yuxiang Factory offered over a hundred bags of Binghua Qing, priced at 10 taels and 0.045 yuan. Huaxin offered over 2,000 bags of spot Dutch red sugar No. 8/9, priced at 9 taels and 4.5 qian. Demand was strong, and all were sold, indicating a vibrant market.

Wufu White Ice Price Increases

Due to hot weather, the Xiamen factory had temporarily stopped production of Wufu white ice, resulting in a scarce supply and low inventory. Recently, limited quantities have been released at a price of 8 taels and 9 qian. According to the factory's telegram, due to rising raw material costs, they plan to increase the price of stored ice by two or three qian before releasing it. Therefore, the market is holding firm, refusing to sell unless the price increases.

Silk and Tea: 30 Bundles of Summer Cocoon Silk Shipped to Hangzhou

This year, the cocoon harvest in various parts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces was poor, with few high-quality cocoons. The summer cocoons produced in Wuxi and other places are only suitable for the domestic silk market. Due to the demand for winter silk, silk merchants have purchased a significant amount of summer cocoon silk from Shanghai factories. Yesterday, 30 bundles were shipped to Hangzhou by the Shanghai-Hangzhou train, purchased by Weicheng Silk Factory as futures contracts.

Factory Yarn Sales Sluggish to Europe

Yesterday, the trading of foreign factory yarn in Shanghai remained sluggish. Currently, domestic silk weaving factories are preparing for their summer holidays. Although they are interested in yellow and white factory yarn, they find the prices too high. Telegram orders have been scarce. Yesterday, only Lianna imported 10 bales of Shanghai white factory yarn, Xinfu imported 15 bales of Shandong yellow factory yarn, and Meida imported 10 bales of yellow coarse silk. Prices remained firm.

Tea Market Continues to Rise

Yesterday, tea merchants from various origin areas showed strong interest in Zhenmei Da Bang green tea from Lai Lu Zhuang, including Yingzhuang, Yihua, Xiehe, Jinlong, and Tianxiang. The market for tea from Wudong, Shexian, and Sui'an was particularly active, with prices soaring by 10 to 20 taels. The prices of tea from Tunxi and Wubei also showed no signs of declining. The Russian Assistance Association has shown great interest in Gongxi, but recently, Baitouzhuang and Huacha Company have been taking the opportunity to acquire the tea. Chinese merchants are holding firm, unwilling to lower prices for sales.

Art World

Death of French Satirical Cartoonist Forain

— Yue Lun

A great loss to the art world recently is the death of the renowned French satirical cartoonist Forain. I regret not being able to immediately travel to Paris to lay a wreath before his spirit. I have specially penned this short article to introduce this deceased artist to fellow art enthusiasts, as a way to mourn him.

At midnight on Friday, the streets of Paris were still bustling. It was at this time that the famous Forain passed away. Accompanying him in death was only his virtuous wife. The patient's moans suddenly turned into cries of grief. The surroundings of the house were filled with a desolate atmosphere. All that remained were the artist's lifetime of work and the few sketches by the artist he admired, Danmier Corat, hanging on the wall.

Forain was born in October 1852. At the age of sixteen, he began studying sculpture under Carpeaux, aspiring to become a sculptor in the future. At the same time, he hoped to achieve greatness in history. It is said that great figures in history often have eccentricities or behaviors that ordinary people consider "strange." Forain was no exception. Consider, Forain was studying sculpture, so why did he later become a famous satirical cartoonist? The story behind this is quite interesting. It turns out that the artist became a painter entirely because of being wrongly accused, which suddenly changed the direction of his studies. It was completely an accidental and unexpected encounter. The story is like this: once, the class monitor unfortunately committed a serious blunder, damaging the right hand of a statue of the Crown Prince made by the teacher's family. The class monitor, fearing punishment, falsely accused Forain of the damage. The teacher, enraged, did not investigate the truth of the matter and abruptly expelled the innocent student from his sculpture studio.

The sudden injustice to the young artist caused him to lose his place of study. Naturally, he felt extremely indignant. As a result of this indignation, he abandoned his original ambition and shifted his interest to the practice of satirical painting. Later, he became the most authoritative satirical cartoonist in modern France. Throughout history, artists or other great figures have often been motivated by injustice to strive in other directions, leading to the creation of great and immortal works or careers. History is full of such examples. Take Qu Yuan of China, for instance. If it weren't for the "senior officials" who "vied for favor" with him and spoke ill of him before King Huai, causing him to be alienated, perhaps our poet would have been an official his entire life and died as such. Where would we have the "Li Sao," passed down for thousands of years, for later generations to recite? From this perspective, perhaps the making of great artists and other great figures requires stimulation. During the European war, our artist served as a soldier, charging into battlefields against the enemy. He even received the Croix de Guerre for his war exploits. Castelman said, "His bravery and will can serve as a model for soldiers."

Speaking of Forain's painting, he is a modern French satirical painting authority, and won the Legion of Honor (La Commandent de la Region I'bonnens). He served as the president of the Satirical Association. In 1923, he was elected as a member of the Academy of Fine Arts, and the chairman of the National Fine Arts Association jury. The British Royal Institute of Oil Painting has hired the director as an honorary member. Fifre, Paris World (Monde' Parisiene), Figaro, French News (Ｃotrier Francaise), Paris Tide (Ech de Paris) Paris Life (La ViaParisien), Journal and other newspapers and magazines often have Forain's works.

The Spanish Literary World After the Success of the Revolution

— Chun

Literature is often the fuse of revolution; this saying is often proven true. Although a considerable number of people oppose the instrumentalization of literature, in a time of emergency, this kind of consciousness cannot be suppressed. The inspiration of writers cannot be immune to the objective social environment, and the people's need for a reasonable life is naturally expressed more urgently in literature. The successful conclusion of this Spanish republican revolution is, of course, no exception. We only need to look at the famous novelist Vicente Blasco Ibáñez's efforts in the revolutionary movement, advocating revolution everywhere, and the powerful exposure and stimulation of revolutionary consciousness in his novels, all of which are enough to prove the Spanish literary world's madness and enthusiasm for the revolutionary movement. Unfortunately, Ibáñez died in exile due to failure, eventually dying in France, without seeing the success of the revolution. However, in recent years, due to the high tide of the revolutionary movement, many people other than Ibáñez have been drawn into the vortex of practical political activities in the Spanish literary world.

The successful establishment of the Spanish Republic has manifested a new life in its political system, and it has also had an extraordinary impact on the literary world. Here, I don't want to talk about the transformation of theory or even the issue of providing goods. What I want to bring up is that after the establishment of the republican government, it immediately dispatched a group of literary writers to serve as ambassadors or ministers to various countries. This is truly unprecedented and perhaps a pioneering initiative, as important countries have almost all been occupied by them. I don't think other countries have appointed diplomats in this way. It is inevitable that this will arouse the envy of the literary world in various countries.

Now, I will write down the names of the people I know below:

1. Novelist, essayist, and poet Ramón Pérez de Ayala, stationed in England.

2. Salvador de Madariaga, famous for popular novels and the most well-known writer in Spain, stationed in the United States.

3. Grejorio Marañón, known for his research on the psychology of the sexes, stationed in France.

4. Renowned philosopher Leso Grttgay Gasset, stationed in Germany.

5. Critic Azorín (real name José Martínez Ruiz), stationed in Argentina.

6. Novelist Smerica Casro, stationed in Cuba.

7. Novelist Miguel de Unamuno, stationed in Cuba.

8. Journalist and novelist Luis Araguistain, stationed in Greece.

9. Historian Rapael de Altamito, stationed in Czechoslovakia.

10. Federico Gorcia Sancbez, whose travelogue novels are rich in both quality and quantity, stationed in Japan.

Literary Miscellany

Louis Lewis Doesn't Want the Medals Anymore

Not long ago, Louis, who had just won the Nobel Prize and was made a laughingstock in the literary world for being slapped in the face, recently lost his temper again and actually wanted to donate the gold medal to Yale University's New Sterling Memorial Library. However, the school authorities treated it indifferently and made no response, which made Louis feel embarrassed and in an awkward position. It is said that this is due to some misunderstanding that has not yet been resolved. Louis can be said to be the unluckiest Nobel Prize winner. (Chun)

The Revival of Portrait Painting

Portrait painting has been largely neglected by the French in the past twenty years, but now there is a trend of revival. Recently, a large-scale exhibition of historical portraits was held in Paris. The purpose of this exhibition is to attract people's attention to portrait painting and to inspire painters to turn to portrait painting and promote the revival of portrait art.

Guidelines for Art Articles

(1) Articles are limited to news, reviews, and introductions about recent art (painting, music, sculpture, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature at home and abroad.

(2) Photos are limited to recent portraits and works of domestic and foreign artists, and various photographs related to art.

Social News

Marshal Foch's Diary of the European War

— Translated by Gu Angruo

Therefore, each army must study the organization of the enemy's rear, to determine whether the enemy has a retreating action, and must always strictly scout the enemy's situation, whether there is a retreating pattern, and must also prepare to pursue, so as to avoid the enemy army having the opportunity to retreat completely.

On July 24th, when the victorious battle in the Tetun area was underway, the Allied commanders-in-chief—Marshal Haig, General Pétain, and General Pershing—gathered at my headquarters in Ponpon to study future plans with me. I asked my Chief of Staff, General Weygand, to read the aforementioned plan to them. The commanders-in-chief seemed startled by the ambition, scope, and frequency of operations in this plan.

The commanders-in-chief gave their respective answers based on their different positions:

Marshal Haig - The British army has been almost completely disintegrated after the battles of March and April, and it will take time to recover.

General Pétain - The French army has been exhausted after four years of fierce fighting, and the soldiers are all suffering from anemia.

General Pershing - The only mission of the American army is to fight, but the American army has not yet been formed.

Under these circumstances, how can our army consider adopting a continuous large-scale offensive?

While acknowledging the rationality of the commanders-in-chief's observations, I insisted on my point of view. I had paid considerable attention to the temporary weaknesses of each army, but I also expected that the proper combination of our army would be sufficient to make the planned implementation possible. In particular, our army can implement it flexibly. What I mean is to determine the speed and slowness of the implementation of this plan based on the current degree of victory.

The commanders-in-chief did not formally express their opposition. When they left me, they each took a copy of the July 24th plan. The next day, they each expressed their agreement in principle. (To be continued)
